\n   <div class=\"container\"> \n        <div class=\"mini-header\">\n        <h2 class=\"grey-header text-center\"><a href=\"learning-and-training-solutions/custom-training/\" title=\"Our Customized Training Solutions\">Our Customized Training Solutions</a></h2>\n        <p>Over the last 16 years, CommLab has developed learning content for a wide range of training programs, applying time-tested instructional design principles and strategies that are a right fit for any type of content.</p> \n           <p>We use the latest generation rapid authoring tools such as iSpring Suite, Articulate
